						"Mana" "%AbilityManaCost"
					}
				}

				"OnOrbImpact"

				"IsHidden"  "1"

				{

				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden"			"0"
			}
			"modifier_hp_shift_datadriven_debuff_counter"  //A visible counter that will appear in Pudge's target's modifier bar.
			{
				"Duration"			"%duration"
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden"			"0"
			}
			"modifier_hp_shift_datadriven_buff"

				"Passive"				"0"
				"IsHidden"  			"1"
				"Attributes"			"MODIFIER_ATTRIBUTE_MULTIPLE"
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_STATS_STRENGTH_BONUS" "%str_bonus_perstack"
				}
				
				"OnDestroy"  //Decrement the visible counter.
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
							  "ScriptFile" "lua_abilities/abilities_simple.lua"
							  "Function" "pudgeHP_shiftBuffOnDestroy"
					}
				}
			}
